name:Tâ€iâ€aâ€nâ€xâ€iâ€nâ€bâ€aâ€oâ€bâ€eâ€iâ€zâ€hâ€u
info:Stayed in April 2024
info:Family
info:15 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted April 21, 2024
msg:I took my parents to Zhenjiang for a weekend trip and stayed at Shuxiang Mansion Hotel. This hotel is located in Xijindu, a historical ancient street in Zhenjiang, and is very close to the famous "Three Mountains" (Jinshan, Jiaoshan, and Beigushan), making it very convenient for travel.
The guest rooms of Shuxiang Mansion Hotel are distributed in Bao's Money House and Yuntai Tower built during the Republic of China period. Mr. Sun Yat-sen once stayed and gave a speech here, with a rich historical and cultural heritage. The guest room facilities are high-end and exquisite, with an antique style, which is exactly what my parents want. The four of us lived in the two-bedroom and one-living room on the ground floor of Bao's Money House. There was a patio at the entrance, which was ventilated and easy to light. The layout of the hall is like a study, with all the four treasures of the study. Dad put down his luggage and spread out the paper and wrote quickly. The hotel front desk was very considerate and said that Hanfu could be borrowed for free. Mom was very happy and immediately borrowed a set of Hanfu to take pictures in the elegant environment.
The breakfast is a set meal for each person (one bowl of pot-lid noodles + one crab meat steamed bun, one fresh meat steamed bun, one vegetable bun, one marinated egg and braised meat, the noodles and steamed buns are freshly cooked) + semi-self-service, with fruits, salads, bread, coffee, pickles, and millet porridge.
The hotel rooms are not only well-equipped, but also warm-hearted, which can be reflected in the details. When guests check in, the service staff will carry their luggage to the room for them, and explain in detail how to use the facilities. The room has already been filled with welcome fruits. In addition, freshly cooked Tremella soup will be delivered in the evening, making people feel at home.

info:Stayed in May 2024

info:1 Review
rating:5
posted:Posted May 13, 2024
msg:We specially chose a room to book after the May Day holiday. The hotel front desk was very considerate. Seeing our family, they took the initiative to help us upgrade the room. Before we checked in, they took the initiative to contact us to reserve a parking space in advance, and they came to pick up our luggage when we arrived at the parking lot. When checking in, they also gave us a detailed introduction to the history of the hotel and the attractions in Zhenjiang, and gave small gifts to the children. The hotel is in a cultural relic protection unit, and all the buildings are from the Ming and Qing Dynasties. The entire courtyard is carved with beams and painted with rafters, with green tiles and red eaves. It is of great historical significance. It is where Mr. Sun Yat-sen stayed and gave speeches. The hotel's breakfast is highly recommended. We booked a breakfast without breakfast at the time, thinking of eating at the scenic spot by ourselves. The hotel front desk recommended the hotel for dining, saying that you can taste all the characteristics of Zhenjiang, pot cover noodles, braised meat and soup dumplings, and other self-service coffee, milk and bread are unlimited. We didn't finish eating with two children, it was very rich. It is a leisure and resort hotel, the service is really amazing, the staff who come in and out will take the initiative to say hello and chat with us, and plan our itinerary reasonably according to our time, which is very nice. We will come again. Thank you for the care of the staff.

name:Aâ€nâ€oâ€nâ€yâ€mâ€oâ€uâ€sâ€ â€Uâ€sâ€eâ€r
info:Tanhua Guestroom (Double bed)
info:Stayed in March 2024
info:Couples
info:35 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted March 21, 2024
msg:It is just opposite the Zhenjiang Museum, with an excellent geographical location. It is a stone's throw away from the Xijindu Scenic Area and is very quiet. This hotel is built in an old house. It is a building complex from the Republic of China period. It has a history of more than 100 years. The entire hotel has only more than 20 rooms and is unique. The hotel itself is a very artistic place. I would like to emphasize that the service is very good, and basically it can meet all requests. It is one of the top three hotels in the country in terms of service. Anyway, it is unexpectedly good. The ladies are very gentle. Yeah. Two tickets to the Xijindu paid scenic spots were also given upon check-in. The bathtub is big enough, and those who like to take a bath will feel very comfortable (but the hotel does not have bath salts, which is very incredible). In particular, the breakfast is very delicious. Their breakfast is not the traditional buffet, but a breakfast for one person, with beef pot cover noodles, crystal braised pork, and one basket of steamed buns per person, the kind with crab roe buns, the remaining milk, soy milk, homemade yogurt, and various pickles, etc. You can take them at the buffet counter. Of course, you can add more if you are not full of staple food. There are beautiful Hanfu at the front desk, which can be used for taking photos. It's free and very clean.
The hotel parking lot is at the back door of the hotel, very close to the hotel, very quiet and safe, and also free.
Overall, it's a good choice to stay in Zhenjiang.
(It should be noted that the wooden structure of the old building may make creaking sounds, which is not very friendly to people with shallow sleep and neurasthenia, but I have neurasthenia and feel okay. On the last day, I met a particularly unrefined guest who got up and screamed at 6 o'clock in the morning. He had no manners at all, which was very annoying.)

posted:Posted March 10, 2024
msg:We stayed at Shuxiang Mansion for a two-day trip to Zhenjiang. The hotel has a superb location. The hotel is within walking distance of Xijindu and Zhenjiang Museum, and is one starting price away from Jinshan and Beigushan attractions. We stayed in the Bao's Money House room, which seemed to have traveled back to the Republic of China. Sun Yat-sen once stayed here. The hotel retains the characteristics of the Republic of China, as well as wood-carved windows and stone-carved floor tiles, which have cultural heritage. Breakfast is a set meal of Zhenjiang pot-covered noodles and soup dumplings, combined with a buffet. The front desk receptionist was very enthusiastic and professional, and patiently introduced the nearby travel guide. When we encountered small problems when parking, they were quickly resolved, which left us with a good impression. I will choose the Shuxiang brand again if I have the opportunity in the future.
